CIDC Data Model

CYTOF Run

Description: Information about the acquisition and analysis CyTOF data for E4412 and similarly formatted trials.

Properties

Property Description Data Type
Inherits all properties from schema: assays.cytof_assay_core
assay_creator
required 		Indicates what site is filling out the assay. assays.components.assay_core#assay_creator
batch_id
required 		CyTOF batch identification number. Unique to every batch. assays.cytof_assay_core#batch_id
participants
required 		< array >
assays.cytof_e4412_assay#participant
assay_run_id User defined unique identifier for this assay run. Not necessarily unique across batches. assays.cytof_assay_core#assay_run_id
cytof_antibodies assays.cytof_assay_core#cytof_antibodies
excluded_samples assays.cytof_assay_core#excluded_samples
acquisition_buffer Cell staining buffer used for antibody and cell dilution. < string >
debarcoding_protocol The strategy/kit used to barcode CyTOF samples, if any < string >
source_fcs < array >
artifacts.artifact_fcs
astrolabe_reports Information about a ZIP file. artifacts.artifact_zip
astrolabe_analysis Information about a ZIP file. artifacts.artifact_zip

Definitions

participant

Property Description Data Type
cimac_participant_id Participant identifier assigned by the CIMAC-CIDC Network. Formated as: C?????? (first 7 characters of CIMAC ID) participant#cimac_participant_id
participant_debarcoding_key An ID that maps to the specific isotope labeling scheme in the debarcoding protocol. < string >
preprocessing_notes Any notes pertaining to preprocessing of CyTOF data. < string >
control A single data record from CyTOF assay batch. < object >
samples < array >
assays.cytof_assay_core#entry
